  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f5486033-9bbc-46ba-8561-2707a602e616'
      });
    }

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1731721014" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18063150190887989121"><b>Death Note, Vol. 3: Hard Run (Death Note, #3), Tsugumi Ohba</b><br/><br/>In order to keep working, Light hides a LCD Mini Television in a bag of chips to see criminals while he writes their names acting as if he is studying. <br/><br/>L decides to remove the cameras, but still suspects Light as a Kira. Some time later, Light enters into the Toho University, where he meets L, who reveals his own identity in order to study Light's reactions. <br/><br/>L reveals to Light that he suspects he is Kira, which forces Light to ally with </span>
  <span id="freeText18063150190887989121" style="display:none"><b>Death Note, Vol. 3: Hard Run (Death Note, #3), Tsugumi Ohba</b><br /><br />In order to keep working, Light hides a LCD Mini Television in a bag of chips to see criminals while he writes their names acting as if he is studying. <br /><br />L decides to remove the cameras, but still suspects Light as a Kira. Some time later, Light enters into the Toho University, where he meets L, who reveals his own identity in order to study Light's reactions. <br /><br />L reveals to Light that he suspects he is Kira, which forces Light to ally with him to prove he is innocent. Soon the channel Sakura TV airs a video from a person with Kira's powers telling people to stop bothering Kira by killing the anti-Kira commentators. <br /><br />Soichiro manages to enter Sakura TV's building with an armored car without being seen, and stops the broadcast. Light notes that the one who made the tapes is an ally for him and that has obtained the shinigami's eyes, allowing him to see anybody's real name and lifespan. <br /><br />After realizing there is another Kira, L requests Light to join them to stop the second Kira. Ohba said that he often struggled while selecting chapter names, but for chapters 15 through 23 he had the titles selected early; he said that he was "on a roll" during that time. ...<br /><br />تاریخ نخستین خوانش: روز بیستم ماه ژانویه سال 2020م<br /><br />عنوان: یادداشت مرگ: کتاب سوم؛ نویسنده: تسوگومی اوبا؛<br /><br />لایت یاگامی، مرد جوانی که از جرم و بزهکاری بیزار است، تصادفاً دفتری پیدا می‌کند که رویش نوشته‌ شده (دفتر مرگ). در صفحهٔ اول دفتر شرح داده شده که اگر نام شخصی در دفتر نوشته شود و نویسنده در همان حال چهرهٔ شخص را در ذهنش مجسم کند، آن شخص پس از چهل ثانیه بر اثر حمله ی قلبی خواهد مرد. «لایت» در صدد استفاده از دفتر برمی‌آید<br /><br />شخصیت‌های اصلی: یاگامی لایت (کیرا)؛ لایت؛ شخصیت اصلی دفتر مرگ، یک پسر بسیار باهوشی است که در حدود هفده سال سن دارد. هنگامی که دفتر مرگ توسط ریوک (یکی از خدایان مرگ)، در دنیای انسان‌ها انداخته شد، لایت اولین کسی بود که به طور اتفاقی با این دفترچه روبرو شده و پی به راز آن می‌برد و شروع به کشتن خلاف کارها می‌کند. مردم به او لقب کیرا (قاتل) می‌دهند، با اینهمه لایت (کیرا) برای پاک کردن پلیدی از دنیا و ساختن آرمانشهر و حکم‌رانی بر دنیای جدید، دست به کشتن انسان‌های فاسد می‌زند و او خودش را عدالت خطاب می‌نماید. لایت که می‌دانست «ال» کارگاه زبردستی است برای اینکه بتواند او را از معرکه خارج کند توسط پدرش که سمت رئیس پلیسی ژاپن را به عهده داشت به «ال» می‌پیوندد و به او در پیدا کردن و دستگیری «کیرا» یاری می‌کند، اما سرانجام لایت با نقشه‌ ای از پیش تعریف شده، توانست «ال» را نیز به قتل برساند غافل از اینکه شخصیت دیگری در داستان وجود دارد که به بعد از مرگ «ال»، با عنوان «ان (نیئر)» در ادامه داستان رونمایی می‌شود و ادامه کار ال را به عهده می‌گیرد و...؛<br /><br />ال: برترین کاراگاه جهان است، او تصمیم دارد که کیرا را ردیابی و دستگیر کند. او فردی شلخته است و خود را در پشت ماسک اسم قرار داده است. در نوع نشستن و لباس پوشیدن، غذا خوردن و...؛ با بقیه شخصیت‌ها فرق دارد. ال می‌دانست که لایت همان کیرا است ولی نمی‌توانست بقیه را به این امر قانع کند و سپس لایت به وسیلهٔ «رِم» که شینیگامی میسا بوده او را به قتل می‌رساند<br /><br />آمانه میسا: دختری که بی‌اندازه به کیرا وابسته است، میسا یک مدل معروف در ژاپن است و علاقه دارد با توجه به کارش لباس‌هایی در مدل‌های مختلف بپوشد. لایت؛ فقط به او به دید یک یاری کننده برای اهدافش نگاه می‌کند، چرا که دفتر مرگ وی و چشمان شینیگامی‌ اش می‌تواند کمک شایانی باشد. قاتل پدر و مادر میسا توسط کیرا مجازات شده و میسا به این دلیل بسیار به کیرا علاقمند است<br /><br />ریوک: شینیگامی که به علت خسته شدن از یکنواختی دنیای شینیگامی دفترچه خود را برای سرگرمی به دنیای انسان‌ها می‌اندازد (دفترچه‌ ای که به دست یاگامی لایت می‌افتد) ریوک بدون جانبداری از هیچ طرف و صرفاً به عنوان تماشاچی به قضیه نگاه می‌کند و تا حد ممکن از یاری به لایت پرهیز می‌کند، ولی در مواردی لایت با استفاده از سیب، که خوراکیِ مورد علاقه ی او می‌باشد، ریوک را مجبور به انجام بعضی کارها می‌کند<br /><br />رم: شینیگامی که به زمین آمد و دفترچه ی خودش را به میسا داد. رم هم مانند ریوک یک دفترچه دارد (دفترچه دوم در واقع متعلق به شینیگامی به نام جلیوس بود که به خاطر اینکه عاشق میسا می‌شود و جان او را نجات می‌دهد کشته می‌شود) پس رم دفترچه را متعلق به میسا می‌داند و شینیگامی میسا می‌شود، سپس به دلیل نوشتن اسم واتاری (یکی از همکاران ال) و ال در دفترچه‌ اش بخاطر نجات جان میسا (طبق نقشه یاگامی لایت) کشته می‌شود<br /><br />ان (نیئر): دوست دوران کودکی ال که شش سال پس از مرگ ال به دستگیری کیرا اقدام می‌کند<br /><br />قوانین: ریوک (یک شینیگامی) در دفتر چند قانون مربوط به طرز استفاده از آن را به زبان انگلیسی نوشته، چون معتقد است که انگلیسی پر سخنگوترین زبان بشری است و هر که دفتر را پیدا کند، روش استفاده از آن را یاد خواهد گرفت<br /><br />تاریخ بهنگام رسانی 25/08/1399هجری خورشیدی؛ ا. شربیانی</span>
  <a data-text-id="18063150190887989121" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer284816266132799181">WHY IS THE 4TH BOOK NOT IN MY HANDS. AHHHH MASSIVE PLOT TWIST AT THE END OF THIS ONE!!! <b>Okay so, as always, I am a fan.</b> (I mean, DUH. I'm on Vol #3, when usually anything that remotely smells like a series takes me 19 years to work through.) I loved this one particularly much <b>because of the sheer amount of deducing and battles of wits.</b> I loooove smart books. This series is SMART. We're talking genius' battling it off and trying to make the other trip up but being so flawless IT NEVER WORKS.<br/><br/>*hype</span>
  <span id="freeText284816266132799181" style="display:none">WHY IS THE 4TH BOOK NOT IN MY HANDS. AHHHH MASSIVE PLOT TWIST AT THE END OF THIS ONE!!! <b>Okay so, as always, I am a fan.</b> (I mean, DUH. I'm on Vol #3, when usually anything that remotely smells like a series takes me 19 years to work through.) I loved this one particularly much <b>because of the sheer amount of deducing and battles of wits.</b> I loooove smart books. This series is SMART. We're talking genius' battling it off and trying to make the other trip up but being so flawless IT NEVER WORKS.<br /><br />*hyperventilates*<br /><br />Guilty confession: Light is a mass murdering teenager and yet I still like him.<br />Less guilty confession: Ryuzaki (or "L") is adorable still and chews on things when he's thinking and has big eyes and I really shouldn't care so much about a little black and white drawing BUT THERE YOU GO.<br /><br /><b>This volume had plenty of plot twists, but it didn't have so much action as more THINKING time.</b> Which I'm okay with. But it did make it slower than the other books, I found. I love that Ryuzaki and Light have MET now and are constantly trying to trip each other up. I feel mortally ashamed of myself for getting panicky about Light possibly getting caught. WHERE ARE MY MORALS? IF YOU FIND THEM, SEND THEM BACK TO ME BECAUSE THIS IS NOT THE TIME FOR A HOLIDAY.<br /><br />(Thank goodness it's library day tomorrow because I need the next ones immediately.)</span>

"L"<br><b><br>First Move (5 Stars)</b><br>Still a Ping-Pong.... and it's getting smarter..<br><b><br>Duplicity (5 Stars)</b><br>Light &amp; L will try to work together!!! but it's not the twist...the twist is how to write an end to this thrilling chapter...<br><b><br>Misfortune (4 Stars)</b><br>Here Light's father will deliver his line of Misfortune, But Will Light accept that?<br><b><br>Hard Run (4 Stars)</b><br>I almost hated it....I'm team Light BUT This chapter he's just went so far....<br>funny he's not here to explain..<br><b><br>Shield (4 Stars)</b><br>Still , had Light gone insane? totally insane? it's "L" chance now to get closer to him.<br><b><br>Fool (5 Stars)<br>Oh my God......We've been fools to believe all of it..<br>It's really big twist..<br><br>I just love how smart the authors are..it's a really great thrilling read.<br><br>Mohammed Arabey<br>from 3 March 2016<br>to 8 March 2016<br><br> </b></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dannii Elle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dannii Elle" href="/user/show/44487975-dannii-elle">Dannii Elle</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44487975-dannii-elle?shelf=fantastic-fabrications">fantastic-fabrications</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44487975-dannii-elle?shelf=artistic-absorption">artistic-absorption</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1639655404" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9478431442033380426">Yet again, another stellar installment of the Death Note series!<br/><br/>This third volume felt more action-packed than its predecessors. The good/bad binaries became even more muddied and the the art work turned darker in tone to accommodate it. It felt like this volume marked a shift in the series, where from here on out we have entered more into the world of the psychological thriller. Again, there were many levels to this and many genres were converged on, but it primarily had a crime-based theme. Th</span>
  <span id="freeText9478431442033380426" style="display:none">Yet again, another stellar installment of the Death Note series!<br /><br />This third volume felt more action-packed than its predecessors. The good/bad binaries became even more muddied and the the art work turned darker in tone to accommodate it. It felt like this volume marked a shift in the series, where from here on out we have entered more into the world of the psychological thriller. Again, there were many levels to this and many genres were converged on, but it primarily had a crime-based theme. This was enhanced by the increasing focus on the police detectives and the mysterious L, who are attempting to solve the case of the homicidal maniac murdering both convicted criminals and the police members attempting to trap him. This insight into the two conflicting sides of the case make this compelling reading!<br /><br />In true Death Note style, this has ended on a cliffhanger that is making it impossible for me to stop now! I am a true convert into the Manga world.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9478431442033380426" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer19598491769662486"><b>3.5 Stars</b> <br/><br/>My favorite of the series so far! <br/><br/>This is such a crazy <i>smart</i> series, and the plot keeps twisting in ways I'd never expect. Light and L are both fascinating characters and it was super interesting getting in both their heads as they face off. <br/><br/>It still moves a little slow at times and I'm not certain what I think overall-- but I'm definitely invested in seeing where this is going. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8887092857452392435"><b>4.5 stars - Spoilers</b><br/><br/>-Liked this more than Volume 2. It was more engrossing and the battle of wits between L and Light was immensely entertaining. <br/><br/>-I didn't expect L to reveal himself to Light, it was a cool twist. I loved seeing them both trying to stay one step ahead of each other. <br/><br/>-The twist at the end was great. I was wondering how Kira/Light was killing off people without knowing their names - I really didn't see the second Kira thing coming at all. <br/><br/>-I'm glad the second Kira was a girl but I</span>
  <span id="freeText8887092857452392435" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars - Spoilers</b><br /><br />-Liked this more than Volume 2. It was more engrossing and the battle of wits between L and Light was immensely entertaining. <br /><br />-I didn't expect L to reveal himself to Light, it was a cool twist. I loved seeing them both trying to stay one step ahead of each other. <br /><br />-The twist at the end was great. I was wondering how Kira/Light was killing off people without knowing their names - I really didn't see the second Kira thing coming at all. <br /><br />-I'm glad the second Kira was a girl but I'm annoyed at how dumb she seems. I also hated that the driving force behind her actions was just so she could impress Kira. <br /><br />-I'm not impressed that all the female characters have either been silly and submissive or have only acted a certain way because of a male character. I don't think it's asking much to have one well rounded female character whose world doesn't revolve around a guy.<br /><br />-Looking forward to volume 4.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14057809562240454171"><b>*I actually read Volume 3 in the Black Editions, but you can't count the volumes separately there so here we are.</b><br/><br/><b><i>"They say humans haunted by Shinigami have nothing but misfortune.”</i> — Tsugumi Ohba, Death Note, Vol. 3: Hard Run</b><br/><br/>One of the best cat-and-mouse games I've ever seen in literature, tbh. Light and L are absolutely brilliant. The tension was high, and the reading experience is addictive! I sat down and finished this in about 1 1/2 hours. Also, <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[the introduction of a second Ki</span></span>
  <span id="freeText14057809562240454171" style="display:none"><b>*I actually read Volume 3 in the Black Editions, but you can't count the volumes separately there so here we are.</b><br /><br /><b><i>"They say humans haunted by Shinigami have nothing but misfortune.”</i> — Tsugumi Ohba, Death Note, Vol. 3: Hard Run</b><br /><br />One of the best cat-and-mouse games I've ever seen in literature, tbh. Light and L are absolutely brilliant. The tension was high, and the reading experience is addictive! I sat down and finished this in about 1 1/2 hours. Also, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the introduction of a second Kira was fucking insane. I am super excited to see what Misa's going to bring to the series. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />However, I feel like outside of the main tension, the characters fell flat. I feel like the characters didn't progress. Light's losing it a little bit more, but everyone just felt stagnant. Also, there are still scenes of casual sexism, which serves no purpose. So why is it there?<br /><br />Volume 2 is still my favorite, but I am so excited for Volume 4!!</span>

        <a title="47Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="47Time" href="/user/show/33626218-47time">47Time</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2283900301" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4596126281690663577">Surprisingly, this volume has some depth to it. On one plane you have L directly involved in checking on Raito who is suspected of being Kira. On another plane you have L's views on Kira and his more aggressive new tactics to lower crime. This comic starts to have similarities to the Columbo tv show in that you know who the killer is and are shown how the investigators discover him.<br/><br/>With his room wired with no less than 64 cameras (how overkill can you get) Raito has to convince L that he isn't K</span>
  <span id="freeText4596126281690663577" style="display:none">Surprisingly, this volume has some depth to it. On one plane you have L directly involved in checking on Raito who is suspected of being Kira. On another plane you have L's views on Kira and his more aggressive new tactics to lower crime. This comic starts to have similarities to the Columbo tv show in that you know who the killer is and are shown how the investigators discover him.<br /><br />With his room wired with no less than 64 cameras (how overkill can you get) Raito has to convince L that he isn't Kira, so he has to kill some people again. You have to appreciate Raito's attention to detail, though L still suspects him based on... nothing. Cause he's Sherlock 2.0. L stalks Raito during an exam and does so with his customary hugging-knees position. L has to sit like that, sucking his thumb, otherwise his investigative abilities are half as effective. You can only find this depth in manga.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[L reveals himself and his suspicions to Raito who can't use the death note to get rid of L as that would make him the prime suspect. What a brilliant plan. A long conversation ensues where L is trying to incriminate Raito and the latter is mostly on the defensive. They are interrupted by a phone call about Raito's father, chief Yagami, who had a heart attack and is in hospital. The chief confirms L's identity to Raito who offers his help for the investigation. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />A tv network gets several tapes from Kira where he outlines his plans for a crime-free world with the police's and L's help. Since they refuse, one of them has to die or else several innocent policemen will die instead. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[L agrees to be the one to sacrifice and uses his spectacular Sherlock-sense to figure out that the Kira who demans this is a different one than the Kira they have been dealing with so far. It turns out the tapes were recorded by a girl named Kira who also has a death note. Raito wants to control the new Kira to clear the real Kira name as much as Kira wants to meet Raito. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

There were a few more heart-in-mouth moments, twists and turns and a great revelation at the end BUT I don't have Vol. 4 so I have to wait for it!! Really love this manga.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('XZrXKK5VRLgleqIktAF4/r61QRezvVr5DNr6fRWcBpJF4rG63V679kqtOHyClyeUzme9Q3fI9B1Yi33oXt9eJw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2Mi+QHRob42odhpmZUksW3dQoypvqaMkwyIdluJ906HAsNjSB2OQw8ehgD5T33MxB4JffqvcDcCXc5oDqT6LFA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer1976721031339153099">Tsugumi Ōba (Profile in Japanese: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/19876928.______' title='大場 つぐみ' rel='nofollow noopener'>大場 つぐみ</a>), born in Tokyo, Japan, is a writer best known for the manga Death Note. His/her real identity is a closely guarded secret. As stated by the profile placed at the beginning of each Death Note manga, Ōba collects teacups and develops manga plots while holding his knees on a chair, similar to a habit of L, one of the main characters of the series.<br/><br/>There is spe</span>
  <span id="freeText1976721031339153099" style="display:none">Tsugumi Ōba (Profile in Japanese: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/19876928.______" title="大場 つぐみ" rel="nofollow noopener">大場 つぐみ</a>), born in Tokyo, Japan, is a writer best known for the manga Death Note. His/her real identity is a closely guarded secret. As stated by the profile placed at the beginning of each Death Note manga, Ōba collects teacups and develops manga plots while holding his knees on a chair, similar to a habit of L, one of the main characters of the series.<br /><br />There is speculation that Tsugumi Ōba is a pen name and that he is really Hiroshi Gamō. Pointing out that in Bakuman the main character's uncle was a one-hit wonder manga artist who worked on a gag super hero manga, very similar to Gamō and Tottemo! Luckyman in all aspects. Also that the storyboards drawn by Ōba greatly resemble Tottemo! Luckyman in style.</span>
